<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chlore</i>, formed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chlorine</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphry_Davy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Humphry Davy">Humphry Davy</a> based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">œáŒªœâœÅœåœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khl≈çr√≥s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cho.html>cho</a> (13678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kweman</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">chuman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwemanƒÖ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kommen.html>kommen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">come</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">koma</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">êåµêåπêåºêå∞êåΩ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***chocolade.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>chocolade</a> (3688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">chocolate</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nahuatl" class="extiw" title="w:Nahuatl">Nahuatl</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> word, though it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not clear precisely which one. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chocolate</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/250px-Chocolate.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="195" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/375px-Chocolate.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Chocolate.jpg/500px-Chocolate.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="934" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>Chocolade</a></i><br />Chocolate</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chocolade.html>chocolade</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>chocolate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the past some dictionaries prescribed a feminine gender, likely because of analogy with <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> that have the ending <i>-ade</i>. This prescription does not seem to have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> any basis in common usage or etymology, however.

<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_Pidgin_English" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese Pidgin English">Chinese Pidgin English</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">ÈÄüÈÄü</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cuk1 cuk1</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to urge someone to do something quickly</span></li></ol>

</p>

<ul><li><b>1977</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Le Carr√©">John Le Carr√©</a>, <i>The Honourable Schoolboy</i>, Folio Society 2010, p. 13:
<dl><dd>‚ÄòAnd another <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>! But <i>cold</i> this time, hear that, boy? <i>Muchee coldee</i>, and bring it <i><b>chop chop</b></i>.‚Äô</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chop-chop.html>chop-chop</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tobacco that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> produced and <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> without excise (tax), and therefore cheap and illegal.

***chow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a> (17692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow-chow.html>chow-chow</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_Pidgin_English" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese Pidgin English">Chinese Pidgin English</a> of unclear origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Food, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a>.
<dl><dd><i>I'm going to pick up some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></b> for dinner.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a>.
<ul><li><b>1914</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Saki"><a href = vnd.unilang:saki.html>Saki</a></a>, ‚ÄòThe Lull‚Äô, <i>Beasts and Superbeasts</i>:
<dl><dd>‚ÄòI'd try and grapple with him myself, only I've got my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></b> in my room, you know, and he goes for pigs wherever he finds them.‚Äô</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1988</b> March 4,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Weinberg,  ‚ÄúFirst Person: <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>Me</a> and Georgia <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Keeffe‚Äù, in  <cite>Chicago Reader</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://securesite.chireader.com/cgi-bin/Archive/abridged2.bat?path=1988/880304/OKEEFFE">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> talking, one of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>, the <a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a> one, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> come <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> and I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> absently petting him.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A Chinese person.
<ul><li><b>1938</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xavier_Herbert" class="extiw" title="w:Xavier Herbert">Xavier Herbert</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capricornia_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Capricornia (novel)">Capricornia</a></i>, Chapter V, p. 74, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/capricornianovel00herb">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>These <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:creatures.html>creatures</a> Nawnim <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> amazed to see about him on the day of his arrival. <li><b>1977</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Le Carr√©">John Le Carr√©</a>, <i>The Honourable Schoolboy</i>, Folio Society 2010, p. 11:
<dl><dd>‚ÄòNow look here old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> if you should ever bump into an interesting <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>Chow</a></b> from <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the river ‚Äì one with <i>access</i>, follow <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>? ‚Äì just you remember High <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>Haven</a>!‚Äô</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">Â∑û</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zh≈çu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A prefecture or district of the second rank in China, or the chief city of such a district.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phono-semantic_matching" class="extiw" title="w:Phono-semantic matching">Phono-semantic matching</a> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">ÂêÉ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chƒ´</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by the ‚Äúfood‚Äù sense of Etymology 1 above.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chow.html>chow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chows.html>chows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:mahjong.html>mahjong</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A run of three consecutive tiles of the same suit.</li></ol>

***christen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a> (6556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cristen</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kersten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ChristiƒÅnus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒßœÅ·øëœÉœÑŒπ·æ±ŒΩœåœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Khrƒ´stiƒÅn√≥s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The current Dutch spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by the Latin and subsequently also the Greek <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:christen.html>christentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">christin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Christian</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerstijndom</i>, with the first element <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> modified to agree with the Latin/Greek spelling. ***chrysalis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a> (94600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">œáœÅœÖœÉŒ±ŒªŒªŒØœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrusall√≠s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">œáœÅœÖœÉœåœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrus√≥s</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">gold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because of the color of some of them.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chrysalises</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chrysalides</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The pupa of a butterfly or moth, enclosed inside a <a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a>, in which metamorphosis <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> place
<ul><li><b>1929</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/M._Barnard_Eldershaw" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:M. Barnard Eldershaw">M. Barnard Eldershaw</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_House_Is_Built" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A House Is Built">A House <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> Built</a></i>, Chapter VII, Section viii
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>Fanny</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> afraid. She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> like an insect new-hatched from its <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></b>, naked and unprotected in a dawn she could not face.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a> itself.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A strong constraint.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">However, with the dainty volume my quondam friend sprang into fame. At the same time he cast off the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></b> of a commonplace existence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chubs</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One of various species of freshwater fish of the Cyprinidae or carp family, especially:
<ol><li>A European <a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a> (<i>Squalius cephalus</i>, syn. <i>Leuciscus cephalus</i>)</li>
<li>in Europe, its close relatives, notably the fallfish.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of various vaguely related marine or freshwater <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a>.
<ol><li>in North America, the black bass.</li></ol></li></ol>

<p>Originated 1890‚Äì95 from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">◊ó◊ï◊¶◊§÷º◊î</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khutspe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Mishnaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">◊ó÷ª◊¶÷∞◊§÷∏÷º◊î</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khutsp√°</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">◊ó÷∏◊¶÷∑◊£</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khats√°f</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be insolent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aramaic" class="extiw" title="w:Aramaic">Aramaic</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">◊ó◊ï◊¶◊§◊ê</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">·∏•u·π£pƒÅ æ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">◊ó÷≤◊¶÷∑◊£</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">·∏•a·π£ap</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be insolent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chutzpahs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Nearly <a href = vnd.unilang:arrogant.html>arrogant</a> courage; utter audacity, effrontery or impudence; supreme self-confidence; exaggerated self-opinion.

***ciao.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a> (10126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Venetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Venetian language">Venetian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">sciavo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in particular the expression <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao vostro</i>, literally meaning "(I am) your slave" but in essence meaning "I am at your service", or "your humble servant"), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sclavus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence also standard Italian <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">schiavo</i>); in the Venetian language originally pronounced <span class="IPA">/st Éa ä/</span>. Development and use <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to the Southern German and Central European greeting of <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">servus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_6">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li>goodbye!
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="it">arrivederla <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:arrivederci.html>arrivederci</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="it">ci vediamo <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>Early 1940s</b>, written by an unknown Italian partisan, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bella_ciao" class="extiw" title="w:Bella ciao"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bella.html>Bella</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>Ciao</a></i></a> (<i>Goodbye, beautiful!</i>):

***cicero.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a> (19688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From its use in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pannartz_and_Sweynheim" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pannartz and Sweynheim">Pannartz and Sweynheim</a>'s 1467 Roman edition of <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>Cicero</a>'s <i>Epistulae ad Familiares</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> to My Friends").<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ciceros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Continental  printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Continental equivalent of the English pica: a measure of 12 Didot points (4.51368 mm or about 0.178 in.) or a body of type in this size.</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>

***cijfer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfer</a> (8862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cifer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cifra</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>digit</li>
<li>statistic</li>
<li>a grade given for an assignment or class, particularly in primary school</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijferen.html>cijferen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cimbaal.html>cimbaal</a> (118795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">simbale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">cimbale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cymbalum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Œ∫œçŒºŒ≤Œ±ŒªŒøŒΩ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k√∫mbalon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Middle Dutch also <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a variant that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from Old French.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cimbaal.html>cimbaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cimbalen.html>cimbalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cimbaal.html>cimbaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cymbal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">percussion instrument</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">klankbekken</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:circus.html>circus</a> (3727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:circus.html>circus</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:citaat.html>citaat</a> (10573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">citƒÅtum</i>, the neutral inflection of the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cit≈ç</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">citƒÅre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cause to move, arouse, summon, urge, call</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the frequentative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cie≈ç</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ciƒìre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, set in motion, stir, rouse, call, invite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> base <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*·∏±ey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move to and fro</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: somewhat equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citeren.html>citeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aat</i>.
